What the heck is an unfunded mandate?  It‚Äôs a federal regulation that requires a state (or local gov‚Äôt) to perform certain actions w/out getting paid for it.  It can also be a reduction/elimination of prior funding for enforcement of such a duty.  #unfundedmandate #purplepatriot
